88w83rhr5v9mx select * from ( select nvl(b.tablespace_name, nvl(a.tablespace_name, 'UNKOWN')) TNAME, round(b.Kbytes_alloc, 2) * 100 KBYTES, round(b.Mbytes_alloc, 2) * 100 MBYTES, round(b.Kbytes_alloc-nvl(a.Kbytes_free, 0)-nvl(c.Kexp_undo, 0), 2) * 100 KBUSED, round(b.Mbytes_alloc-nvl(a.Mbytes_free, 0)-nvl(c.Mexp_undo, 0), 2) * 100 MBUSED, round(nvl(a.Kbytes_free, 0)+nvl(c.Kexp_undo, 0), 2) * 100 KBFREE, round(nvl(a.Mbytes_free, 0)+nvl(c.Mexp_undo, 0), 2) * 100 MBFREE, round(((b.kbytes_alloc-nvl(a.Kbytes_free, 0)-nvl(c.Kexp_undo, 0))/ b.Kbytes_alloc)*100, 2) * 100 PCIUSED, round(((nvl(a.Kbytes_free, 0)+nvl(c.Kexp_undo, 0))/ b.Kbytes_alloc)*100, 2) * 100 PCIFREE, round(nvl(a.K_largest, 0), 2) * 100 KLARGEST, round(nvl(a.M_largest, 0), 2) * 100 MLARGEST, round(nvl(b.Kbytes_max, b.Kbytes_alloc), 2) * 100 KMAXSIZE, round(nvl(b.Mbytes_max, b.Mbytes_alloc), 2) * 100 MMAXSIZE, round(decode(trunc(b.Kbytes_max/b.Kbytes_alloc, 0), 0, 1, (b.Kbytes_alloc/b.Kbytes_max)*100), 2)* 100 PCIMAX, nvl( ts_fragment_number, 0) TSFGNUM, round(decode(trunc(b.Kbytes_max/b.Kbytes_alloc, 0), 0, round(((nvl(a.Kbytes_free, 0))/b.Kbytes_alloc)*100, 2), ((b.Kbytes_max-b.Kbytes_alloc+nvl(a.Kbytes_free, 0))/b.Kbytes_max)*100), 2)* 100 PCIFMAX from ( select sum(bytes)/1024 Kbytes_free, sum(bytes)/1024/1024 Mbytes_free, max(bytes)/1024 K_largest, max(bytes)/1024/1024 M_largest, tablespace_name, count(tablespace_name) ts_fragment_number from sys.dba_free_space group by tablespace_name ) a, ( select sum(bytes)/1024 Kbytes_alloc, sum(bytes)/1024/1024 Mbytes_alloc, sum(decode(autoextensible, 'NO', bytes, 'YES', maxbytes))/1024 Kbytes_max, sum(decode(autoextensible, 'NO', bytes, 'YES', maxbytes))/1024/1024 Mbytes_max, tablespace_name from sys.dba_data_files group by tablespace_name) b, ( select sum(bytes)/1024 Kexp_undo, sum(bytes)/1024/1024 Mexp_undo, tablespace_name from sys.dba_undo_extents where status = 'EXPIRED' group by tablespace_name) c where a.tablespace_name (+) = b.t ablespace_name and c.tablespace_name (+) = b.tablespace_name order by 1 ) where ((((MMAXSIZE > :BindValue0) AND (MMAXSIZE <= :BindValue1) AND (PCIFMAX <= :BindValue2) AND (TNAME NOT LIKE :BindValue3)) OR ((MMAXSIZE > :BindValue4) AND (MMAXSIZE <= :BindValue5) AND (PCIFMAX <= :BindValue6) AND (TNAME NOT LIKE :BindValue7)) OR ((MMAXSIZE > :BindValue8) AND (PCIFMAX <= :BindValue9) AND (TNAME NOT LIKE :BindValue10) AND (MMAXSIZE <= :BindValue11))) )AND (ROWNUM<= :maxrownum)

PGA Aggr Target Stats

  • B: Begin Snap E: End Snap (rows dentified with B or E contain data which is absolute i.e. not diffed over the interval)

  • %PGA W/A Mem - percentage of PGA memory allocated to workareas
  • %Auto W/A Mem - percentage of workarea memory controlled by Auto Mem Mgmt
  • %Man W/A Mem - percentage of workarea memory under manual control

  • Note there is often a 1:Many correlation between a single logical object in the Library Cache, and the physical number of memory objects associated with it. Therefore comparing the number of Lib Cache objects (e.g. in v$librarycache), with the number of Lib Cache Memory Objects is invalid.

Interconnect Ping Latency Stats

  • Ping latency of the roundtrip of a message from this instance to
  • target instances.
  • The target instance is identified by an instance number.
  • Average and standard deviation of ping latency is given in miliseconds
  • for message sizes of 500 bytes and 8K.
  • Note that latency of a message from the instance to itself is used as
  • control, since message latency can include wait for CPU
